  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_42b9aa30-e958-4d2e-8418-66b3459d7d2d'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer15063111233101298785"><i>Librarian's note: An alternate cover edition can be found <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35006073.here' title='here' rel='nofollow noopener'>here</a></i><br/><br/><br/>BOOK THREE: TRISTAN & DANIKA <br/>THE IMPACT <br/>Tristan hit rock bottom, and no one felt the impact harder than Danika.   <span id="freeText15063111233101298785" style="display:none"><i>Librarian's note: An alternate cover edition can be found <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35006073.here" title="here" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a></i><br /><br /><br />BOOK THREE: TRISTAN &amp; DANIKA <br />THE IMPACT <br />Tristan hit rock bottom, and no one felt the impact harder than Danika. She was forced to see, in the most brutal of ways, that love does not conquer all. Bruised, bloody, and broken she had to walk away. <br />THE AFTERMATH <br />Picking up the pieces of your life after a tragedy is a daunting prospect, and that’s considering you still own all of the pieces. But what if you don’t? What if someone else owns those pieces, and those pieces are a part of your soul? <br />You dig deep and work with what you’ve got. <br />That’s what Danika told herself and believed, every single day, for years. <br />Tristan and Danika’s love had failed every test that life had thrown at them. She couldn’t forget that, not for one second. And if those tests had been overly harsh, well, she wasn’t one to wallow in self-pity. The failure was the thing she had to focus on. The failure was the lesson. She had no intention of working so hard to make it out of hell without learning that lesson well. <br />THE REUNION <br />Over six years after the night that changed everything, Danika finds herself forced to spend the weekend constantly in Tristan’s company, as they attend the wedding of two of their dearest friends. It’s been long enough that she feels they can be friendly again without it destroying her peace of mind, but just a small amount of time in his presence has her remembering something she had forced herself to forget: There’d been a reason she’d gone through hell with this man, for this man, some true good to precede the bad. <br />She shocks herself by quickly giving in to a hunger that she never imagined could still consume her. <br />Even the best intentioned denial has a breaking point. <br />THE HARSH REALITY <br />After everything that’s happened, the rise and the fall, the pain and the aftermath, can these two navigate the waters of acute regret, survive the trials of coming face to face with all that they have lost, and find the strength to try again? <br />This book is intended for readers 18 and up.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15063111233101298785" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

 I was planing to read Up in the air series after I finish this one but after I read about the colar and touching thing I changed my mind. Weird couple .</a>

<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/60028318-jade-violet"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1585268947i/60028318._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/60028318-jade-violet">Jade Violet</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">He does allow some people. But NOT Jackie or Tristan because they're dominants too and it goes against the rules of their lifestyles. Danika is free t<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">He does allow some people. But NOT Jackie or Tristan because they're dominants too and it goes against the rules of their lifestyles. Danika is free to touch her.<br /><br />The collar around the neck is commitment and ownership. While she is his wife and equal, they also have a dominant/submissive relationship. The collar represents her being his submissive and also permanent commitment to each other only.<br /><br />Up in the air has more bdsm and is less angsty. I liked it though - he's never been in love before and most of his actions through the entire trilogy are based on the fact that just like his dad said about his mother 'when you know, you know straight away'. His pursuit of Bianca is one of chemistry and sexual attraction but it's also much more deeply rooted in being hit by 'The One'. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/769306666?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer769306666" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12871080695569620697"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394691309i/8890506._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/679269.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>**** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ****<br/><br/><b>What a beautiful ending to Tristan & Danika's story!!</b><br/><br/>If you love second chance romance, this is a must-read series! In this final instalment of the <em>Tristan & Danika</em> trilogy, R.K. Lilley truly brought this love story full circle. From the first time I met Tristan and Danika's characters in the <em>Up In The Air</em> trilogy, I've loved them and been intrigued by their story. What could have happened to make two people who so clearly loved each other become <em>so</em> estranged? And</span>
  <span id="freeText12871080695569620697" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394691309i/8890506._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/679269.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>**** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ****<br><br><b>What a beautiful ending to Tristan &amp; Danika's story!!</b><br><br>If you love second chance romance, this is a must-read series! In this final instalment of the <em>Tristan &amp; Danika</em> trilogy, R.K. Lilley truly brought this love story full circle. From the first time I met Tristan and Danika's characters in the <em>Up In The Air</em> trilogy, I've loved them and been intrigued by their story. What could have happened to make two people who so clearly loved each other become <em>so</em> estranged? And, would they ever find their way back to each other after hitting rock bottom? ... In this trilogy, all our questions were answered as we were taken through the highs and lows of Tristan and Danika's tumultuous, heart wrenching, and passionate relationship.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I'm Tristan. I am an alcoholic and a drug addict. I'm here because using cost me the love of my life."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I won't go into too much detail about the plot but there is some of it that isn't a secret because, when we saw Tristan and Danika in the <em>Up In The Air</em> books, we knew that they spent years apart. In the first book of this series, we saw the love and passion that brought them together, in the second book, we found out the cause of their tragic separation, and in this last book, we discovered what took place during those six years apart and what finally happened to bring them back together.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I longed to have her in my life. In any capacity. I'd literally take anything. I wouldn't be happy with less than everything, but I'd take what I could get."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Taking us year by year throughout their separation, we got to see how they coped, how they dealt with the pain, what they felt, what they did, and where their hearts still lay. I loved how, despite all the bad that happened to them, and despite everything that came between them (even if those things were sometimes their own actions), neither of them every truly stopped loving the other.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"How can you still love her so much?..."</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"Because that's how love works. It doesn't die, even when you don't feed it. That's just the way it is... Loving her has become a part of who I am."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Even though their separation was painful, I also understood it and I loved how they never truly lost their connection... and when the healing <em>finally</em> began, I just couldn't stop smiling.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Whatever you need me to be, I'll be that. Whatever you want me to do, however we need to make this work, we will do it."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Everything was realistically paced -- never rushed -- and throughout it all were these undercurrents of the kind of passion that only comes from true once-in-a-life time love tempered with the reluctance that only comes after immense heartbreak. Their was not an easy path and my heart went out to them as they slowly rebuilt everything that had been broken. They were both fighting their respective battles and it was both painful and heartwarming to see Tristan work <em>so</em> hard to regain Danika's trust and to see her want to trust him but be understandably wary of putting her heart out on the line  again.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Love doesn't let you walk away clean. Love is messy…. Love takes a fucking piece of you before it's done."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>At the end of the day though, despite all the pain and heartache, there was no doubt that they really were perfect for each other and seeing them happy just had me smiling for pages on end. I loved their teasing, their banter, their games and private jokes, their passion, their love... everything.<br><br>Tristan and Danika were just one of those couple who you <em>knew</em> were meant to be together. I was proud of them honestly. I'd seen them at their best and at their worst, I'd seen them both mature and heal and finally find their way back together. I was wiping happy tears by the end. It really was a beautiful, heart-melting end to their story.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Oh sweetheart. You haven't been paying attention…. I am the guy who has been in love with you for over six fucking years. I am the guy who has thought about you every day. I miss you every day. What happened -- what we lost together -- breaks my heart, but it doesn't change anything."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I think that second chance romances are some of the most powerful ones because not only do you have an epic love but you also have the first hand knowledge of what it's like to have lost that love... so when it's found again, you can't help but treasure it.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"You were not responsible for making me worse. But I'll tell you one thing, it's a fact that you were responsible for making me better."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I absolutely adore RK Lilley's writing. I've loved every single book I've read from her. Her characters and their stories just draw you in and you can't help but be feel invested in their lives. She's one of my favorite authors and I highly recommend all her books for anyone who loves hot, passionate, addictive romance.<br><br>4.5 stars<br><br>*******************************<br><br><blockquote>
  <strong>TIMELINE CLARIFICATION</strong>
</blockquote><br><br>The <em>Tristan &amp; Danika</em> trilogy is a spin-off of the <em>Up In The Air </em>trilogy (in which we first met Tristan and Danika as side characters). Both trilogies can be read on their own though and you don't <em>need</em> to read them both to understand the stories. However, their timelines are interconnected.<br><br>The first 2 books of this trilogy, <em>Bad</em> <em>Things</em> and <em>Rock</em> <em>Bottom</em> take place 5 years before <em>In</em> <em>Flight</em> (the first book in the <em>Up In The Air </em>trilogy). Then, chronologically, come the three books of the <em>Up In The Air</em> trilogy.... and then finally comes <em>Lovely Trigger</em> (the last book in the <em>Tristan &amp; Danika</em> trilogy).<br><br>So chronologically, this would be the order of the books:<br><br>✦ Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika #1)<br>✦ Rock Bottom (Tristan &amp; Danika #2) - <em>starts right after Bad Things</em><br>✦ In Flight (Up In The Air #1) - <em>starts 5 years after the end of Rock Bottom</em><br>✦ Mile High (Up In The Air #2)<br>✦ Grounded (Up In The Air #3)<br>✦ Lovely Trigger (Tristan &amp; Danika #3) - <em>starts </em><i>6 years after the end of Rock Bottom </i><br><br>However, the suggested reading order is to read all 3 <em>Up In The Air</em> books, and then the <em>Tristan &amp; Danika</em> trilogy. Trust me, it all works out very clearly :)<br><br><br>*******************************<br><br>Here's my casting for Tristan &amp; Danika:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410623i/805391.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410623i/805393._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>****************************<br><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br></b></span>

<div id="review_743538479" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/743538479" />
    <a title="Mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22667925-mia"><img alt="Mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406604077p2/22667925.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743538479?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mia" href="/user/show/22667925-mia">Mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=sob-fest">sob-fest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=forever-favs">forever-favs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=reread-worthy">reread-worthy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743538479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15442204363077734874"><blockquote>Love is not about<i> want... </i><br/>Love is not about<i> good... </i><br/>Love doesn’t let you walk away <i>clean... </i><br/>Love is<i> messy... </i><br/>Love takes a fucking piece of you before it’s done. <br/><br/><b><i>If it is ever even possible to be done.</i></b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428425283ra/14420582.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I don’t think I could ever come up with more perfect words to describe Tristan and Danika’s love story, or as Danika jokingly called it: <b>
  <i> The great war of T&D.</i>
</b> Their love was just that –a war. It was a long, tortuous, all-consuming fight full of battles and victories, defeats and triumphs, tra</span>
  <span id="freeText15442204363077734874" style="display:none"><blockquote>Love is not about<i> want... </i><br>Love is not about<i> good... </i><br>Love doesn’t let you walk away <i>clean... </i><br>Love is<i> messy... </i><br>Love takes a fucking piece of you before it’s done. <br><br><b><i>If it is ever even possible to be done.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428425283ra/14420582.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I don’t think I could ever come up with more perfect words to describe Tristan and Danika’s love story, or as Danika jokingly called it: <b>
  <i> The great war of T&amp;D.</i>
</b> Their love was just that –a war. It was a long, tortuous, all-consuming fight full of battles and victories, defeats and triumphs, tragedies and trials.<br><br>This may be the longest review I have ever written, but I honestly think I could talk about my favourite book couple forever. Seeing their story come to a conclusion was bittersweet, but it was the most satisfying ending I could have asked for such an incredible series.<br><br>This book picks up where the last left off. The first few chapters span the 6 years of little to no communication between Danika and Tristan, both in their own quiet suffering. Their lives are exactly where they wanted to be, only missing one crucial detail –each other. Neither one can truly move on, so when circumstances call for them to be reunited, Tristan knows he need Danika back in his life. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “We needed to become best friends again. Yes, that was how I would do it. I needed to become so essential in her life that she couldn’t conceive walking away. <br>I meant to break her.<br>Needed to break her.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>He knows getting Danika back is no easy task and first he’ll have to break down the walls she spent years putting up. Danika and Tristan have never been ones to do anything half-assed and when reunited, their love and history all comes back full-fledged with a one way ticket on the crazy train.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394580458ra/8874198.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>To say that I cried from the first page to the last would be no exaggeration of any sorts! But they weren’t all bad tears, not at all. I cried tears of happiness and sadness, of heartache and laughter. Tears of nostalgia and memories, of reunions and regrets. Tristan and Danika’s story was one of hope, loss, and <i>second chances.</i> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “You don’t need to follow every impulse in life; you don’t need to take on every gamble. But some, even ones that have burned you before, well, some of them you do. Some of the sweetest moments in life come from second chances.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>Those first few chapters were so hard to read but so necessary. So many second chance books go straight to the big reunion, but I liked how unrushed Danika and Tristan's was. We got to see their lives year by year and the struggles they went to in their attempts to move on from one another. But like Danika said, with a love like theirs, is it even possible?<br><br>Tristan and Danika are two of my favourite book characters. Neither is perfect. They both have flaws and edges and there were times throughout these books when I wanted to shake them both, but I love them nonetheless. They are fighters; they are survivors. Neither was dealt an easy hand at life or love, but they fought and fought and fought. I could not think of any two more deserving characters of such a perfect ending.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Because that’s how love works. It doesn’t die, even when you don’t feed it. That’s just the way it is. I wouldn’t change it, even if I could. Loving her has become a part of who I am.”<br></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>One thing you can always count on this author for in her books is the steam. Her sex scenes are steamy and sexy, and Tristan left me fanning myself as always! His new kinky side was as intense as ever and I loved every page. The chemistry and spark between him and Danika has always been on fire, and RK Lilley did not fail to deliver in this one.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383713604ra/6641837.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is a fine line between showing a character’s growth and change, and making them into a whole new unrecognizable person. I absolutely hate when authors completely change a character in the middle of series just for the sake of the story, but RK Lilley kept each character in these books true to who they were from the very beginning. <br><br>My heart broke for the young and in love Tristan and Danika we had met so long ago but I found myself falling in love with them, falling in love with <i>their love</i> all over again.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“I knew she still loved me. I could see it now, even if she was still in the throes of denial. She didn’t have to say it in words. She spoke to me in so many other ways. Her love spoke to me in every surrendering line of her body. <br>It spilled out of her pure silver eyes every time she looked at me. <br>She was mine again. <br>And, even when she hadn’t wanted me, when I’d lost all faith, I’d always, <i>always </i>been hers”</b>
</blockquote><br>Of course, Danika and Tristan changed so much throughout their years apart, but I loved that even through those drastic changes, we could see the wrenching similarities of the young characters we fell in love with so long ago. <br><br>I felt so nostalgic every time something from the first book was mentioned and pretty much burst into tears whenever they talked about Jared or 'the lost years'. I was bawling when Tristan was staring at Danika in that diner, comparing the girl he once loved to the woman before him. <br><br>I most loved seeing the change in Tristan. He’s a character I love so much and feel so invested in. My heart broke in the second book, seeing him become just a shell of the man he had once been. In this book, he was healthy and sober, but still the adorable, caring, cocky bastard we fell so hard for.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Mine, my lips told her...<br>Mine, my body told her, as I pinned her to the wall...<br>Mine, my heart cried out to her.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394578881ra/8874050.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The amount of humor in this book was such a pleasant surprise. RK Lilley had me clutching my middle and laughing out loud with silly things like the cinnamon challenge, dick pics, pussy ring tones and (of course) Tristan’s magic hands. <br><br>She planned the series so well and each book balanced the other out. Bad Things was all sweet and sexy, Rock Bottom was an emotional train wreck, and Lovely Trigger was the perfect conclusion to these much deserving characters. I laughed to the point of tears again and again! It felt so good to see Tristan and Danika happy again. From the very beginning, the way they talked like best friends, their banter and playfulness was what had won my heart. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “In my whole life, there are only two people that I’ve ever called my best friend.” <br>My eyes filled from his raw tone as much as his words. <br>“You and Jared.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394578881ra/8874051.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “You make me happy. You know that, right?” <br>“Don’t,” I said weakly. <br>“Don’t what? Be happy? I can’t help it when you’re in my life.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I love all these books so much and fell for each character, and not just our beloved D&amp;T. I loved seeing James, Bianca, Frankie, Estella, Bev, Jerry, Stephan, Javier, Lana, Akira… each character holds such a special and unforgettable place in my heart. Their perfect ending really is more sweet than bitter, because I know this is a series I will return to again and again!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394303557i/8833543._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a>Book 1 review</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/681425839?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Book 2 review</a><br><br>Read in March 2014<br>Reread: August 2014<br>Reread: August 2015<br>Reread: Feb 2020</span>
  <a data-text-id="15442204363077734874" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743068628?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=third-time-s-the-charm-romance">third-time-s-the-charm-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-love-my-friends">i-love-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=panty-dropping-hot">panty-dropping-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=alpha-heroes">alpha-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=top-rated">top-rated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743068628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3875797163665463810"><b>4.5+ EXPLOSIVE STARS</b><br/><br/>Wow! *wipes tears* I don’t think I’ve read about a couple like Tristan and Danika who so deserves their happily-ever-after! This third and final book concluding the trilogy is everything I hoped for! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394594856i/8875512._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>To be honest, I almost didn’t read this book. After the emotionally devastating (and that’s really an understatement) events from book 2 I didn’t think I was strong enough to read more of Tristan and Danika’s pain and regrets. Rock Bottom actually made me believe that these two w</span>
  <span id="freeText3875797163665463810" style="display:none"><b>4.5+ EXPLOSIVE STARS</b><br><br>Wow! *wipes tears* I don’t think I’ve read about a couple like Tristan and Danika who so deserves their happily-ever-after! This third and final book concluding the trilogy is everything I hoped for! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394594856i/8875512._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To be honest, I almost didn’t read this book. After the emotionally devastating (and that’s really an understatement) events from book 2 I didn’t think I was strong enough to read more of Tristan and Danika’s pain and regrets. Rock Bottom actually made me believe that these two would never get their HEA because of past tragedies and I just <i>couldn’t</i> accept that if it were the case in book 3. But holy flying cow! Guys, this book…it definitely wasn’t perfect, and as the reader looking in from the outside I disagreed with some of the character’s actions, but hell, it was <i>perfect</i> for Tristan and Danika. It was their beautifully broken story of how they slowly started to heal and entertained the idea of giving their love a second chance.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394594856i/8875513._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First and foremost, I <b>LOVED</b> the setup of the book and how RK Lilley paced the story. I’m usually not a fan of time gaps, but it was done so well here. These characters, particularly Danika, had gone through hell and back and I could 1000% understand that it’d take years, maybe even a decade, for old wounds to heal. I really appreciated that the author didn’t just jump dramatically to 6 years later or a decade later. Instead, she paced out their story so every year or so, I’d get a glimpse of how Tristan and Danika were doing, an update on their healing progress, and to me, that helped me accept the possibility that they <i>could</i> get together again. <br><br>Before, Tristan and Danika as a couple were dysfunctional, poisonous, and slowly tearing each other apart so I expected to see some development or improvement on each side to making their relationship work, and I did! It was immensely gratifying to see Tristan take up responsibility and he worked <i>so</i> hard to earn back Danika’s trust and love: some of his tactics had me giggling and sniffling over the thoughtfulness and tenderness in which he held Danika in regards to. And Danika…as much as she tried to protect herself from <i>feeling</i> again, there was never any chance of denying her feelings for Tristan. They were bound to happen and even if R.K. Lilley didn’t have them meet up 6 years later, should it be a decade later or 20 years later, their meeting and second chance is inevitable. These two people are just meant for each other. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394594856i/8875514._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's extremely rare for me to connect with two characters on such a deep level and that is the case with Tristan and Danika's story. I started out reading this series to get more glimpses of James and Bianca but instead I finished this trilogy with the thought that these books have well surpassed the Up in the Air books! Complete love and respect for this author!<br><br><b>SERIES READING ORDER</b><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17377032.Bad_Things__Tristan___Danika___1_" title="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1371404883s/17377032.jpg" alt="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> Sorry, no review but TRUST ME and read it please! <a href="http://amzn.to/1hOgd41" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18943009.Rock_Bottom__Tristan___Danika___2_" title="Rock Bottom (Tristan &amp; Danika, #2) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1385363364s/18943009.jpg" alt="Rock Bottom (Tristan &amp; Danika, #2) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/677769827?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">MY REVIEW</a> <a href="http://amzn.to/1gGSqRo" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18681461.Lovely_Trigger__Tristan___Danika___3_" title="Lovely Trigger (Tristan &amp; Danika, #3) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1384923832s/18681461.jpg" alt="Lovely Trigger (Tristan &amp; Danika, #3) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://amzn.to/1dK89jP" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><br>P.S. The author used many personal experiences in this book so if you haven't already, I encourage you all to read this heartfelt <a href="http://rklilley.com/blog/2014/3/3/just-a-quick-note-on-perspective-and-well-cancer-the-c-word-yeah-i-said-it" rel="nofollow noopener">BLOG POST</a> <br><br><b>For more reviews, freebie lists, &amp; giveaways visit my blog!</b><br><a href="http://bookvigilantereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_743157336" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/743157336" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743157336?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743157336" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12103806567256896716"><b>5 fabulous stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/f0c40d1b-79e9-49c6-be32-ad2cee93cc34_zps0af1f487.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394788286i/8906507.jpg' alt=' photo f0c40d1b-79e9-49c6-be32-ad2cee93cc34_zps0af1f487.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I am a huge fan of R.K. Lilleys. Every book of her’s I’ve read, I’ve loved. The <i>Up in the Air</i> trilogy is a favorite of mine, but after completing <i>Tristan & Danika’s</i> series, I have a new favorite. Book two left me distraught. I have been waiting for this book, for the answers and closure I needed. I was not disappointed. It was the perfect conclusion to this series. <br/><br/>Tristan and Danika’s relationship was not easy. In fact, it was destructive at times. The two were madly in l</span>
  <span id="freeText12103806567256896716" style="display:none"><b>5 fabulous stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/f0c40d1b-79e9-49c6-be32-ad2cee93cc34_zps0af1f487.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394788286i/8906507.jpg" alt=" photo f0c40d1b-79e9-49c6-be32-ad2cee93cc34_zps0af1f487.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I am a huge fan of R.K. Lilleys. Every book of her’s I’ve read, I’ve loved. The <i>Up in the Air</i> trilogy is a favorite of mine, but after completing <i>Tristan &amp; Danika’s</i> series, I have a new favorite. Book two left me distraught. I have been waiting for this book, for the answers and closure I needed. I was not disappointed. It was the perfect conclusion to this series. <br><br>Tristan and Danika’s relationship was not easy. In fact, it was destructive at times. The two were madly in love, and they were best friends. Now, after everything, they are nothing to each other. Tristan picked up the pieces of his life and got it back in order. He wants Danika in it whatever way he can have her. Even though she doesn’t want him in her life, it doesn’t stop him from loving her. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/2ea9bf1c-fc98-4cf8-aaf3-be042bb4786c_zps8ebb2603.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394788286i/8906508.jpg" alt=" photo 2ea9bf1c-fc98-4cf8-aaf3-be042bb4786c_zps8ebb2603.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It took Tristan losing everything that was important to him to truly get his life together. <br><i>
  <blockquote>I’d been torn apart and put back together, and though I knew the end result was better now than who I’d been before, somedays it didn’t feel that way. Lots of days, it just felt like the world had lost it’s color, and the only things that defined my life were the things that I’d lost.</blockquote>
</i><br><br>Then there is Dankia. Danika was left broken. Broken hearted and trying to get through and realize that this is her reality. Even though she forgives Tristan for all the wrongs he’s done, she can’t have him in her life. Forgiving is one thing, forgetting she will never be able to do.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/6119f890-04c4-4609-a78a-03f6a829c250_zps9cd78bc5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394788286i/8906509.jpg" alt=" photo 6119f890-04c4-4609-a78a-03f6a829c250_zps9cd78bc5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The first part of the book was hard to read. It took us through both of their lives during the six years they were apart. It hurt to see them both hurting. With everything that happened, they needed that time. Six years later, they are thrown together at a wedding. They know it’s there, that spark and connection they’ve always felt for one another. It’s never left. When Danika is around Tristan, it just feels right. <br><i>
  <blockquote>It felt right. Like I was coming home. Every single time. That’s how this felt. Tristan and I were entering a new and unfamiliar chapter, only it didn’t feel that way. It felt like no time had past at all.</blockquote>
</i> <br>Danika comes to realize what Tristan has always known. They need each other in their lives. Even if it is just friendship. The problem is that all those other feelings are in the way. Getting hurt once makes it so hard to put yourself out there again. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/0df3ca03-ea9b-40bf-806b-7fda1a045028_zpsba77ba0e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394788286i/8906510.jpg" alt=" photo 0df3ca03-ea9b-40bf-806b-7fda1a045028_zpsba77ba0e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It’s not easy, but Tristan works for it. He’s willing to go as slow as Danika needs. Do whatever it takes to win back her trust and friendship, and hopefully in the end, more. <br><br><br>Tristan stole my heart in this book. Anything he’d ever done in the past was forgotten. His love for Danika was powerful. He knew she was the love of his life, the only one for him, and he was never letting her go again. I loved how persistent he was, but not too pushy. He knew what she needed. He was willing to fight for her and he did. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I feel so lost.” <br>He took my hands in his. “Not anymore. I’m right here. I’ve got you.” <br>“There is this hollow place inside of me, where my faith in you used to be. I am so full of fear, and I do not know how to let myself trust you again. I don’t have the strength to do this. Not again.” <br>“I’ve got enough for both of us.” He moved closer, wrapping me in his arms. <br><br>“I don’t know how I even did it,” said Tristan softly. “Looking back from here, I have no idea where I found the strength to let you stay out of my life for so long.”</blockquote>
</i><br> <a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/4a005632-8d1d-4625-8b55-15b47922c33f_zpsec750846.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394788286i/8906511.jpg" alt=" photo 4a005632-8d1d-4625-8b55-15b47922c33f_zpsec750846.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story had everything I love- second chance romance, love, steam, and even some humor thrown in. I was pleasantly surprised to have a few laugh out loud moments. <br><i>
  <blockquote>The bed reminded me of a lifestyle. <br>It reminded me of Frankie. <br>“It was Frankie and James, wasn’t it? Did those kinky fucks bring you over to the dark side?” <br><br>“Tristan Vega: Thanks for accepting my friend request . I promise to try my hardest to refrain from sending you too many dick pics.”</blockquote>
</i><br><br>After finishing this trilogy and the Up in the Air trilogy, I feel like I need to clear something up. <br><br><u>Retraction from previous review of Bad Things, written June 13th, 2013:</u><br>Some of you may remember me making this statement at the beginning of my review- <br><i>
  <blockquote>Now, Tristan was no Mr. Cavendish, but he was pretty damn close.</blockquote>
</i><br>I’m a big enough person to admit when I was wrong, and I’m saying it now. I was wrong. After reading <i>Lovely Trigger</i>, I’ve come to the conclusion that Tristan is just as wonderful as Mr. Cavendish, maybe even more so. He completely redeemed himself for any past mistakes. He was PERFECT. ♥<br><br><br>I enjoyed this book immensely. No other couple deserved love and happiness more than Tristan and Danika. Their love story is destructive at times, but powerful, emotional and beautiful. Their story solidifies that some people truly belong to one another. <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Oh sweetheart. You haven't been paying attention…. I am the guy who has been in love with you for over six fucking years. I am the guy who has thought about you every day. I miss you every day. What happened -- what we lost together -- breaks my heart, but it doesn't change anything."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/0054b848-03b4-43ed-8592-f25db8e6c8bb_zpsdc3625c9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394788286i/8906512.jpg" alt=" photo 0054b848-03b4-43ed-8592-f25db8e6c8bb_zpsdc3625c9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743536892?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743536892" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7763183673226329231"><b>5+ all-of-me-loves-all-of-you stars! </b><br/><br/>Lovely Trigger begins just a few months after the accident and spans the next six years while pivoting back and forth from Danika and Tristan’s point of views.<br/><br/>Danika is trying to pick up the pieces after the accident and move on. She tried her best. She tried to be enough to save Tristan, but in the end she had to <s>walk</s> crawl away. Broken and bruised.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394560889i/8871326.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I never cried a tear of self-pity. That had never been my poison. Bitter was my poison, and it took ev</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText7763183673226329231" style="display:none"><b>5+ all-of-me-loves-all-of-you stars! </b><br><br>Lovely Trigger begins just a few months after the accident and spans the next six years while pivoting back and forth from Danika and Tristan’s point of views.<br><br>Danika is trying to pick up the pieces after the accident and move on. She tried her best. She tried to be enough to save Tristan, but in the end she had to <s>walk</s> crawl away. Broken and bruised.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394560889i/8871326.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I never cried a tear of self-pity. That had never been my poison. Bitter was my poison, and it took every ounce of character I possessed not to let it consume me.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Tristan knew he needed to find sobriety. In the mess that became his life after losing Jared, the baby and the feeling of Danika slipping through his fingers; his rock bottom shot up from beneath his feet and consumed him. <b>Ruined him. </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394560889i/8871327._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> It was the most bitter pill to swallow; how my own rock bottom had impacted her. I had always been the one to throw myself in front of a punch for my brother, my mother. <br><br>And my wife. My wife. I’d have done anything to take her pain, to bear her injuries myself. Instead though, I caused them.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394560834i/8871320.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>When James &amp; Bianca’s wedding forces these two together, they both try their best to not allow their history to cloud the beautiful day for their two friends. But these two don’t just have a history, they have explosive chemistry that can’t be controlled and in most cases can’t be denied. <br><br>Six years have passed since they lost everything. Six years of Danika trying to move on and failing to ever let anyone else consume her heart, six years of Tristan being sober and trying lose himself in women; only to find that nothing took the pain away. <br><br>But something changes, Tristan held her for a moment and felt her and knew that he wanted all of her, but would be willing to take any piece she offered. Her being so close, in the same city, working in the same casino wasn’t enough. He knew that she’d let him in, even if just for a few moments – but he knew he’d have to break down her walls to get there.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I meant to break her.<br>Needed to break her.<br><br>Whether it be with deceit, subterfuge, cold calculation, or sheer will power alone, I was set in my course.<br>She’d built a wall up against me. A wall that seemed to me to be interwoven in to her very soul.<br>For years, I thought that wall was impregnable. But a few words, a few brief encounters had shown me that the wall wasn’t stone, but glass.<br><br>I meant to break it, and her, and anything that stood in my way. I was going to shatter all of the things she used to keep us apart.<br><br>It had become my sole purpose. And if she failed to give, to yield, I”d break myself in the process.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394560834i/8871321._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Tristan and Danika didn’t just have a horrible break up in their past to deal with. His sobriety taught him to face his demons and to accept the things that resulted of his actions. Danika spent six years grieving for a loss that wasn’t one of just a moment in time, but one that would scar her for the rest of her life. While Tristan had to push through to break free, Danika shoved her fears down, drowning them out while trying to move on – only to resurface later.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381945866i/5456817._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I loved this series, these characters. I loved them all from the moment I met them and I have laughed and cried with them over the the last year. R.K. Lilley did an utterly breathtaking job creating this story. I am not sure if this was always their story or if bits and pieces came to life as she wrote it, but it was one helluva story in the end. <br><br>I can’t recall a character that I’ve been more drawn to, that I felt more soundly before, than Tristan. His emotions were always so in your face and on display that you couldn’t help but become completely consumed by them. When Tristan was happy, I smiled – boy did I smile... but when he was hit with the harsh reality of what their past held, I cried. One moment of him breaking sent me spiraling. It didn’t matter if I was laughing the second before, the minute his pain was visible... I felt it. I can’t recall the last time I read a book where that feeling was so evident, so persistent. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394560834i/8871322.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I wanted this story to have a happily ever after, I needed it to. I knew that no matter whatever the final scenes held that there would be pain felt along the way. And that part that was settled between the start of this book and the final words did not disappoint. <br><br>We were given closure as to what happened with that letter that Tristan never got... how that could have impacted their future. We found out if our instincts about Dahlia were correct or not... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I could see where she was coming from, but there is no understanding or forgiving what a piece of shit sister she was.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>The one thing that I loved about Danika from the start of this series was that although she always had cause to be insecure because of the man Tristan used to be and the way people were drawn to him; she rarely fed that monster. Oh, what I wanted to do to that bitch, Mona. <i>You know that classic magician trick where the assistant gets sawed in half? Well I wanted that trick, but I also wanted something to go horribly wrong. No second compartment where someone else’s feet dangled out of the end... nope. Just her and one helluva accident....</i><br><br>I never wanted to see two characters fight harder for what they deserved. Not just half measures filled with good intentions. To really fight, dirty if needed – but to fight hard. Their romance started out as a battle. We knew going into this series that they didn’t survive. We read Bad Things, falling in love with them deeply – wondering how something so powerful could crumble. We went into Rock Bottom knowing that our world was going to shatter. But with Lovely Trigger we were going to finally get a future. No more of the story of their past, but a story born from the ashes of their destruction. Although this method killed me, I absolutely loved it. Knowing that they were apart, and going back to seeing how it all began only to know it wasn’t going to last – but never being able to give up hope. That is what this author gave us. So many times during Rock Bottom I wanted a different ending, knowing that it wasn’t possible. But I just could not let it go. Lovely Trigger gave me every moment I needed. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Somewhere, in the great expanse of space,<br>There is a home where soul reside,<br>Yours and mine were joined together<br>I have not moved from that place,<br><br>God help me, I’ll never move from that place<br><br>But there was a poison in my heart,<br>And darkness in my mind<br>I wasn’t there when you were drowning<br>Though I’d give my soul to take it back<br>You had to leave me behind<br><br>You had to leave me behind<br>How did you leave me behind? </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394560834i/8871323._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And we get heat. The combination of these two have always been explosive, even destructive. That hasn’t changed. Whether a HEA lies in their future or if they are just opening up the scars of their past, there is no doubt that these two burn up the pages of this story. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394560834i/8871324._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>One of the things I loved the most about R.K’s writing is the way she gives you little warnings of things to come. Some may say, hey that was awful nice of you to prepare us a bit for what’s to come... but oh, no those warnings are not nice. Those little warnings aren’t meant to give you time to brace yourself... but in Rock Bottom those things drove me to tears and when I stumbled across that very same little trick in Lovely Trigger my only thought was ‘and this is why I fucking love her books’ – <br><br>I loved every second of this journey that originally started in first class on an airplane, eventually landed on an island in Hawaii and suddenly found its home on the strip in Vegas. For me, these could never just be stand-alone stories of the characters that could be read independently. This was a group of characters that claimed a part of my heart that I will gladly let them keep. <br><br><br><br>=========pre-review=========<br><b>Not one, not two, but THREE</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385425706ra/7146646.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Early 2014? Do you promise R.K.?</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385425706ra/7146647.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But what shall we do until then?</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385425706ra/7146648.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="7763183673226329231" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_743172664" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/743172664" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743172664?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743172664" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer352302503264997710">★★★★★ <b>5+ WONDERFUL, TOUCHING SECOND CHANCE STARS.</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"Some of the sweetest moments in life come from second chances."</i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394883178i/8920034.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If I could give this book more than 5 stars I would... No amount of stars will ever be enough to express my love for this series. Tristan and Danika's story is one that will definitely stay with me for a very long time and it will from now on reside on my all-time-favorites shelf.<br/><br/><b>'The saga of Tristan and Danika' -<br/><i><blockquote>The battles and the victories.<br/>The defeats and the triumphs.<br/>The trage</blockquote></i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText352302503264997710" style="display:none">★★★★★ <b>5+ WONDERFUL, TOUCHING SECOND CHANCE STARS.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Some of the sweetest moments in life come from second chances."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394883178i/8920034.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If I could give this book more than 5 stars I would... No amount of stars will ever be enough to express my love for this series. Tristan and Danika's story is one that will definitely stay with me for a very long time and it will from now on reside on my all-time-favorites shelf.<br><br><b>'The saga of Tristan and Danika' -<br><i><blockquote>The battles and the victories.<br>The defeats and the triumphs.<br>The tragedies and the trials.</blockquote></i></b><br>I laughed, I cried, I swooned, I wanted to punch certain people in the face and others I wanted to give a hug. I went through so many emotions while reading this series and even though book 2 left me heartbroken, by the end of Lovely Trigger my belief was restored and I once again felt like I could finally breathe.<br><br><b><u>WARNING:</u> this review contains SPOILERS for those who have not read book 1 &amp; 2 in the series.</b><br><br>Lovely Trigger starts off with Danika and Tristan each going their own way. After the accident at the end of Rock Bottom, Danika made the decision to stay far away from Tristan because bad things happen when they stay together. She's decided to move on with her life and focus on her career. Tristan, after leaving rehab, still struggles with his bad habits but he's determined to become a better person.<br><br>He wants Danika back, and even though she wants nothing more to do with him, his feelings for her have never changed.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i><b>"How can you still love her so much? She won't even talk to you."</b><br>"Because that's how love works. It doesn't die, even when you don't feed it. That's just the way it is. I wouldn't change it, even if I could. Loving her has become part of who I am."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394893060i/8921093.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Over the course of six years, we follow Danika and Tristan's journey that occasionally overlaps. Whenever they meet though<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Love doesn't let you walk away clean. Love is messy. I don't have to tell you, of all people; Love takes a fucking piece of you before it's done."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The author had done an incredible job at making the story detailed enough without ever making it too long or ever becoming dull. The fact that it was written in dual POV also helped me understand the characters and what they were going through much better and so I was glad for those alternating POV's.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394893060i/8921094.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"We needed to become best friends again. Yes, that's was how I would do it. I needed to become so essential in her life that she couldn't conceive walking away. <br><b>I meant to break her.<br>Needed to break her."</b></i>
</blockquote><br>T &amp; D still have the best chemistry whenever they're together. Despite everything that happened, being friends comes natural to them and it was fun seeing them fall into old habits. Tristan still loves torturing and challenging Danika with his bets, nicknames and magic tricks and the fact that they so easily pick things up where they left off when it comes to their friendship, shows just how perfect they are for each other.<br><blockquote>
  <i><b>"In my whole life, there are only two people that I've ever called my best friend."</b> My eyes filled from his raw tone as much as his words. <b>"You and Jared."</b></i>
</blockquote><br>Slowly but surely, their friendship evolves into something more, but Danika still keeps a tight lid on her feelings. She's afraid of opening up and making herself vulnerable again. Her trust in Tristan was destroyed, which is perfectly understandable considering what happened, but Tristan is determined to restore what they had. The fact that he fought so hard to win her back made me love him even more than I already did. &lt;3<blockquote>
  <i>"I am the guy who has been in love with you for over six years. I am the guy that has thought about you every day. I miss you every day. What happened - what we lost - breaks my heart, but it doesn't change anything. I still want to marry you, and I still want you to be the mother of my children."</i>
</blockquote><br>Still, their journey towards happiness is not an easy one and they have much more obstacles to overcome. Tristan and Danika are both such strong characters and the fact that they've both overcome so much and still try to make the best out of the hands they've been dealt made their story all the more admirable and powerful. Of course, there were also some less favorable characters in the story such as Twatalie who still kept showing up, Mona, Dahlia, Danika's dad...but overall the side characters helped make the story even better and it was fun catching up with James and Bianca, Lana and Akira and Frankie and Estella throughout the years.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394893060i/8921095.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I couldn't have wished for a more perfect ending to this EPIC saga... Once I started reading it, I could NOT put it down until I reached the very end. And let me tell you, losing a few hours sleep over it was 100% worth it. The only downfall is that now that it's over, I feel a huge book slump coming up...what will ever compare to the magnificence of this story? (That might sound a bit over-dramatic, but I'm actually serieus, lol.) <br><br>Overall, R.K. Lilley has done an amazing job and even though I already loved her work based on the Up in the Air-series, I have now become an even bigger fan!!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394899751i/8921957.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>♫ <i>"Somewhere, in the great expanse of space,<br>There is a home where souls reside,<br>Yours and mine were joined together,<br>I have not moved from that place,<br><br>God help me, I'll never move from that place."</i> ♫</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394967927i/8930599.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Series reading order:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17377032.Bad_Things__Tristan___Danika___1_" title="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1371404883s/17377032.jpg" alt="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537960850?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> / <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Bad-Things-Tristan-Danika-1-ebook/dp/B00CX3F2QY/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1394967162&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=bad+things" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18943009.Rock_Bottom__Tristan___Danika___2_" title="Rock Bottom (Tristan &amp; Danika, #2) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1385363364s/18943009.jpg" alt="Rock Bottom (Tristan &amp; Danika, #2) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/656150414" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> / <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Rock-Bottom-Tristan-Danika-2-ebook/dp/B00GW9K8EG/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1394967235&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=rock+bottom" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18681461.Lovely_Trigger__Tristan___Danika___3_" title="Lovely Trigger (Tristan &amp; Danika, #3) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1384923832s/18681461.jpg" alt="Lovely Trigger (Tristan &amp; Danika, #3) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Lovely-Trigger-Tristan-Danika-3-ebook/dp/B00IX51J2C/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1394967266&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=lovely+trigger" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><a href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394736264i/8898096.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer887644607" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2102420084770731033"><b>FOUR LOVE IS MESSY STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I'd keep trying forever, if I had to, to make her trust me again."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395410350i/8992030._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I've had a love-hate relationship with this trilogy from the start, but one things for certain the Tristan and Danika series is undeniably unforgettable. There's been love, lust, heartbreak, tear out your hair angst, knicker twisting sheet clenching sexy times and enough up and downs to satisfy any fair ground ride junkie. RK Lilley has a speciality for making her readers feel every possible emotion a</span>
  <span id="freeText2102420084770731033" style="display:none"><b>FOUR LOVE IS MESSY STARS.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"I'd keep trying forever, if I had to, to make her trust me again."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395410350i/8992030._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've had a love-hate relationship with this trilogy from the start, but one things for certain the Tristan and Danika series is undeniably unforgettable. There's been love, lust, heartbreak, tear out your hair angst, knicker twisting sheet clenching sexy times and enough up and downs to satisfy any fair ground ride junkie. RK Lilley has a speciality for making her readers feel every possible emotion and after the highs and lows of this series I'm glad to say that I made it through all three books ... Just about, here's the rest of my 'lovely trigger' review thoughts.<br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>'Lovely Trigger' is the third and final book of the 'Tristan and Danika' series by RK Lilley. The trilogy is designed to be read in order and this book is the conclusion to a love story and the hope of a happy reunion. Tristan and Danika fell in love with a passion that was all consuming, their love was undeniable and explosive. Neither of them could imagine or believe what they would have to go through and they would never foresee that they may have to consider a future without each other. When tragedy strikes and life is not as they had dreamed they both have to find the strength to move forward to a life of belief that there has to be hope. As Tristan and Danika navigate through life picking up the broken pieces, they have to find a way to move on from the past or say goodbye forever.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396038355i/9081067._SX540_.jpg" width="405" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396038355i/9081068._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>No one can say that this book isn't entertaining and hold-on-your-kindle-this-is-one-hell-of-a-ride-addictive. Any author that can hold the attention of Goodreads like RK Lilley has with this this series deserves recognition. Love it or hate it, I don't think any reader can deny that this series was like a compulsive addiction and once I started that first page of the trilogy I needed to know what would become of this insanely obsessive but strangely loveable couple. After all that had happened to get me to the third and final book of the series ultimately meant that I was invested in seeing a second chance at love that would hopefully blow my socks off. By the time I got to the last page I can admit that I wiped away a tear and had the biggest and goofiest smile on my face. The journey to a happily forever was well worth the wait of finally getting to the ending and I'm glad to say that I fell in love with Tristan and Danika's love once again. This book has some wow moments that made me have that squeeze your heart feeling and it's worth mentioning that I went a little highlight crazy, this author has a way with words that quite frankly is magical. Danika and Tristan have taken up residence in that part of my heart that is reserved for characters that jump on the train of crazy love and I wouldn't have had them any other way.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396038355i/9081069._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396038355i/9081071._SX540_.jpg" width="405" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Why not five?</b><br>Following on from book two in the series I struggled to forget about the difficulties that Tristan and Danika faced, sadly I found that I was still reeling from the over dramatised actions and conclusion of this couples relationship from book two. Having said that I was excited to finish up the series in what I'd heard to be an amazing finale. For the first quarter of the book I really felt I was connecting to the possibility of reconciliation between Danika and Tristan but as the book progressed towards the middle I started to feel like the book was largely repetitive and at that point I was feeling like I liked the book but I was nowhere near in love and I had settled to give this book a three star rating. Then I was presented with the ending of this trilogy and I was blown away, RK Lilley delivered the perfect ending and my book heart was left more than happy.<br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>This series will drive you to distraction, make you fall in and out of love more times than you thought possible, break your heart, mend your heart and take you on a journey that is simply unforgettable. There were parts that I will treasure and moments that I wish I could forget, but one thing that I am certain of is that RK Lilley is an author that is not to be missed, the 'in flight' series is one of my favourites and I'm not a little bit afraid to admit to my stalking of future releases to come. If you love your stories to be full of drama, outright obsessive love and heartbreak then you do not want to miss out on the trilogy, go grab it readers. Enjoy, kisses.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396038355i/9081070._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="2102420084770731033" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
