<div id="review_743095029" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/743095029" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743095029?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743095029" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17225280208705753730">The second book, <i>Rock Bottom</i>, well...left us on rock bottom reeling from all the drama, hurt and pain that Danika and Tristan went through. But...there has to be hope that somehow, someway these two can find their way back...and to each other. <br/><br/>This is the <i>final</i> chapter in Tristan and Danika's journey. I feel like I've been waiting forever for it but I was so hesitant to read it and for it be done, over, finite. Of course, there was no way I could hold back and thank goodness, I didn't. It was <b>A-</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17225280208705753730" style="display:none">The second book, <i>Rock Bottom</i>, well...left us on rock bottom reeling from all the drama, hurt and pain that Danika and Tristan went through. But...there has to be hope that somehow, someway these two can find their way back...and to each other. <br><br>This is the <i>final</i> chapter in Tristan and Danika's journey. I feel like I've been waiting forever for it but I was so hesitant to read it and for it be done, over, finite. Of course, there was no way I could hold back and thank goodness, I didn't. It was <b>A-MA-ZING</b>!!!<br><br>I love ~both~ Tristan and Danika...how could you not? Especially after being through their journey of such wonderful highs and such horrible lows. I have to admit, I wasn't sure they could make it. But they both have grown sooo much and isn't life about <b>
  <i>second chances</i>
</b>? <br><br>One thing I do know is that the sex scenes are scorching!! There are no holds barred with those two...anytime and anywhere! ;) I definitely loved having both POVs especially with these scenes. I loved reading how much they were both affected. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394679936i/8888545.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And not only are we dealing with some drama from Tristan and Danika but we have secondary characters having their own dramas. There's a lot going on... <br><br>♦ Mona - what a witch but we all saw that coming. <i>(and she was just plain out creepy!)</i><br><br>♦ Dahlia - still being a brat. I had higher hopes but I did like how things ended up. <br><br>♦ Bronson - Danika's Dad...can we all just say "eeewwww"<br><br>♦ Dermot - I like how that worked out. <br><br>♦ James &amp; Bianca - of course, I still love them and how things are going for them. <br><br>♦ Lana &amp; Akira - they were pretty funny and sweet.<br><br>♦ Frankie &amp; Estella - loved how Frankie was there for ~both~ Tristan and Danika. And how could you not love that ending? <br><br>♦ Stephan &amp; Javier - both incredibly sweet. would love more about them. <br><br>♦ Bev - it was hard reading what happened but if I didn't already love her, I definitely would now. <br><br>Sooo...did Tristan redeem himself? Well, of course, I can't tell you that but I will say that I was happy to see him struggle and to find out how much things affected him. Thank Goodness for his POV...the book would not be the same without it! And I loved how he worked his "magic". <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394679999i/8888555._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm really sad it's over. This is seriously a series I could reread and would definitely recommend it. I think I almost like it better than the Up in the Air series. Blasphemy I know! LOL! <br><br><b>
  <u>Recommendation:</u>
</b><br><br>If you're looking for an intense love affair with lots of angst, drama and sexy times, this is the series for you. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>❤A big shout out to Melissa for doing a BR w/me...it was great having you to discuss things with! xxoo ❤ </i>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298441ra/683859.gif" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b> <br><br>♥ "Sometimes protecting your heart is the only way to keep your sanity.”<br><br>♥ "Now make like a magician and disappear.” <br><i>(Corny I know but it made me giggle when Danika said it.)</i><br> <br>♥ “Fuck.  Well, <i>that</i> messes with my head.  What can I do to convince you to let me see that again?”  He smiled.  “I barely got a glance.  If I’m going to be fantasizing about that tonight, it would be nice to have a very clear picture.”  <br><br>♥ “It was Frankie and James, wasn’t it?  Did those kinky fucks bring you over to the dark side?” <br><br>♥ “<i>Love</i> doesn’t let you walk away clean.  Love is <i>messy</i>.  I don’t have to tell you, of all people; Love takes a fucking piece of you before it’s done.”  <br><br>♥ “If I’d had even an ounce of hope left that you would let me so much as kiss your fucking feet again, I would have <i>waited for you</i>.” <br><br>♥ “You don’t need to follow every impulse in life; you don’t need to take on every gamble.  But some, even ones that have burned you before, well, some of them you do.  Some of the sweetest moments in life come from second chances.” <br></span>

</a><br><br>Book three begins a few months after Danika's accident, and Tristan and Danika are separately trying to pick up the pieces of what's left of their lives. They are both lonely, but trying to move forward, and heal from their devastating break up.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/0556caf3-3cc1-4cc0-b06c-9fa5ddf3b911.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Tristan really has come a long way. After Danika's accident he hits rock bottom. He's lost everyone that has ever mattered to him, all because of addiction. He comes to terms and accepts responsibility for destroying his relationship with Danika, and realizes his alcohol and drug addictions have cost him the love of his life.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/5208f3fb-076f-4464-9324-8dbf13963dc7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394748551i/8900465.jpg" alt=" photo 5208f3fb-076f-4464-9324-8dbf13963dc7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tristan knows his life is completely out of control, and unmanageable, and seeks help. He goes to rehab, and starts seeing a counselor, and attending group therapy. He starts to deal with his demons, and make changes to better his life.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/f99faed6-da00-4cee-a0a2-e354802e1802.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394746292i/8899832._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo f99faed6-da00-4cee-a0a2-e354802e1802.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tristan is now staying clean, but has so many regrets. He is heartbroken at how he impacted Danika's life. He is obsessed with getting her back, and showing her he's changed. He is willing to do whatever it takes to have her in his life, and will take whatever she can give, even if it's just friendship.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/8b7d900e-61ae-4291-baee-e5a193955235.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394746292i/8899833.jpg" alt=" photo 8b7d900e-61ae-4291-baee-e5a193955235.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tristan and Danika both work at the Cavendish Casino in Vegas. Tristan is a magician at the theatre there, and Danika runs the art gallery. When they see each other it is awkward, and Danika is still bitter, and tries to avoid him as much as possible. They both try to date others, but their hearts are always elsewhere. They can't either seem to find anything or anyone that comes even close to what they shared together.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/41e51e14-7955-4ec3-866a-f19482c8945f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394749816i/8900707._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 41e51e14-7955-4ec3-866a-f19482c8945f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Six years after their break up they both attend a friends wedding, and are in the wedding. They still both miss and long for each other. Being in close quarters sparks ignite, and the explosive chemistry they've always shared can't be denied when they touch.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/f06343e7-35ff-4b54-a10f-387f6ecd2c29.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394749816i/8900708.jpg" alt=" photo f06343e7-35ff-4b54-a10f-387f6ecd2c29.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>They return to Vegas, and decide to try being friends, and begin to hang out occasionally. They start to feel comfortable with each other again, and find themselves really enjoying each other. They communicate well, and Danika starts to see how different Tristan is now, and quits fighting her feelings for him.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/59ff0549-1030-482c-8372-91fd2b4bdb7e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394746478i/8899910._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 59ff0549-1030-482c-8372-91fd2b4bdb7e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really adored this whole series. It really takes you on a journey. It is a roller coaster of emotions and at times was hard to get though, but so worth it in the end. It was one of the hottest series I've read! <br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/4a059e68-7687-40d5-a917-d64cff11751d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394746666i/8899971.jpg" alt=" photo 4a059e68-7687-40d5-a917-d64cff11751d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There are so many wonderful things to love about Tristan Vega! He is flawed, and makes a lot of mistakes, but gets himself together, and makes changes. He is a beautiful man inside and out. A huge teddy bear of a guy, with such a loving, tender heart! He is also passionate, sexy, and did I mention he is a fabulous cook, &amp; he's in a band. :D Yes, I think I'm officially in love with Tristan Vega! :)) Had a blast reading this series with Sharon! I enjoyed talking Tristan with you &amp; having someone to vent to! lol &lt;333<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/a2a3f566-826f-4996-be6a-775fcca9fae6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394746666i/8899972.jpg" alt=" photo a2a3f566-826f-4996-be6a-775fcca9fae6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-My body did not want to leave her any more than my heart did. I did not know how I was going to move on, but it was clear that she already had.<br><br>-How had it come to this? I had the clearest picture in my head, of the way she used to look at me, like I was her whole world. I would have given anything to have that back.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/4c04c956-5511-4e2b-8888-218014f579e7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394751755i/8900968.jpg" alt=" photo 4c04c956-5511-4e2b-8888-218014f579e7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-Lots of days, it just felt like the world had lost its color, and the only things that defined my life were the things I'd lost.<br><br>-His thick eyelashes cast deep shadows on his passion-slackened face, just the tiniest hint of his eyes visible to mine. But it was enough. I loved to see that look in his eyes, even if it did drag me back in time six years, to when I'd believed that love could conquer everything.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/70514679-33b3-4d8f-aae9-697436b96cd0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394751755i/8900969.jpg" alt=" photo 70514679-33b3-4d8f-aae9-697436b96cd0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-It was all happening again. Every insane fucking bit of it was back. The all-consuming infatuation. Back. The tight pull in my chest every time I looked at him. Back. Falling asleep in his arms and still dreaming about him. Back. Insane psychotic jealousy. Back. Doubly, because we were both afflicted with it. Public make-out sessions, as though we were teenagers. Back. Vibrating tongue and magic hands that made me lose all brain function. Back. The heaven and hell of being with a man I couldn't stand to be parted from for even and hour. Back. His smile ruining me for every other smile in the world. The joy and the pain of being undeniably, unquestionably in love.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/5a7ec669-0042-401f-b4bc-6aa45f1b37c1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394754255i/8901355.jpg" alt=" photo 5a7ec669-0042-401f-b4bc-6aa45f1b37c1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-Her love spoke to me in every surrendering line of her body. It spilled out of her pure silver eyes every time she looked at me. She was mine again. And, even when she hadn't wanted me, when I'd lost all faith, I'd always, always been hers.<br><br>-Because, whether she would admit it or not, every time we gave in to this hunger, this unforgiving passion, we showed our true feelings to each other. She couldn't give herself to me without showing me her vulnerability, and I couldn't take her without revealing my utter devotion, my forever love.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/1e74c595-08f5-4d30-baf4-18d4d7b4f124.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394754255i/8901356.jpg" alt=" photo 1e74c595-08f5-4d30-baf4-18d4d7b4f124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-I laid my head on his chest as he kissed the top of my head. I could have stayed there forever. It felt like coming home.<br><br>-"You don't need to follow every impulse in life; you don't need to take on every gamble. But some, even ones that have burned you before, well, some of them you do. Some of the sweetest moments in life come from second chances."<br><br></span>

<div id="review_769502780" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/769502780" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/769502780?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer769502780" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11556874563733715145"><b>5 Compelling Stars!</b><br/><br/><b>Mild spoilers ahead!!</b><br/><br/>After the heartbreaking events of Rock Bottom which broke my heart and left a bad taste in my mouth, I was apprehensive as to how RK Lilley is going to take this story and give the readers a satisfying and believable HEA. Because honestly, it's so hard to come back from those horrifying events in Rock Bottom. But she pulled it off and gave one of my most beloved couple the HEA they deserved!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“Some of the sweetest moments in life come from second chances.</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText11556874563733715145" style="display:none"><b>5 Compelling Stars!</b><br><br><b>Mild spoilers ahead!!</b><br><br>After the heartbreaking events of Rock Bottom which broke my heart and left a bad taste in my mouth, I was apprehensive as to how RK Lilley is going to take this story and give the readers a satisfying and believable HEA. Because honestly, it's so hard to come back from those horrifying events in Rock Bottom. But she pulled it off and gave one of my most beloved couple the HEA they deserved!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Some of the sweetest moments in life come from second chances.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Lovely Trigger picks up where Rock Bottom left off; Danika and Tristan living separate lives. The story slowly unfolds as both Danika and Tristan deals with the aftermath of their actions a year, two, three and then six years after where the bulk of the story takes place. Everything has changed. For Tristan, the enormity of what happened finally hit him and he was so remorseful and so full of guilt. For Danika, it was a battle not to let bitterness consume her. She had lost everything in the aftermath of the Great War of T&amp;D. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“I never cried a tear of self-pity. That had never been my poison. Bitter was my poison, and it took every ounce of character I possessed not to let it consume me.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Their reunion didn't happen in an instant. It took over the course of six years before Danika can even acknowledge Tristan's presence, and years more for them to finally talk. But when they finally got together...<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/WDUG7fP" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422603ra/841109.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But it was also sad and heartbreaking. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/CRlvP46" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388399765ra/7823718.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But it also had some funny moments. Dick pics anyone? <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/o86KGVA" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394806986ra/8908636.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Still their road to healing was bumpy with Danika still doubting herself and Tristan. I felt that it took her longer to heal emotionally because she lost so much because of her relationship wtih Tristan. I can totally understand where she was coming from having lost everything. A lesser man would have balk and just leave things as they are but not Tristan. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Oh, sweetheart. You haven’t been paying attention … I am the guy who has been in love with you for over six fucking years. I am the guy that has thought about you every day. I miss you every day. What happened — what we lost together — breaks my heart, but it doesn’t change anything.”</b>
</blockquote> <br><br>He totally owned it. Tristan is relentless is his pursuit of Danika. He slowly but surely wormed his way right back into her good graces, her affection, and her pants - and not necessarily in that order. Boy, did he ever! I was so rooting for him at the same time wanting to see him suffer a bit. Danika's defenses didn't stand a chance.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“I feel so lost.”<br>He took my hands in his. “Not anymore. I’m right here. I’ve got you.”<br>“There is this hollow place inside of me, where my faith in you used to be. I am so full of fear, and I do not know how to let myself trust you again. I don’t have the strength to do this. Not again.”<br>“I’ve got enough for both of us.” He moved closer, wrapping me in his arms.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>He totally won me over again and again. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/J3WPQkd" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435911ra/880863.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lovely Trigger is the book that restored my faith in trilogies. Just a little bit. I'm still leery of them but if every trilogy is as compelling and heartrending as this one, I will wait and read each one of them. Yes, it has a lot of angst. And yes, the main characters often make mistakes. But Tristan and Danika's story resonated in that love is often messy and heartbreaking but still deserving of a second chance. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Love is not about want.<br>Love is not about good.<br>Love doesn’t let you walk away clean.<br>Love is messy.<br>Love takes a fucking piece of you before it’s done.<br><br>If it is ever even possible to be done.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/mF6pOAE" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394806986ra/8908637.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11556874563733715145" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743098405" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11512287836410949535"><b>4.25 Second Chance Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394745176i/8899606._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>He'd set me adrift, so very long ago, and I had wandered into deepest waters, with depths far too vast for me to navigate alone.<br/>And here he was, swimming out to save me. Had he been following me all the while? Had I been so blind?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394745176ra/8899607.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>What a perfect conclusion to the trilogy. It was emotional, angsty, erotic, everything you would want in a book. I waited until book 3 was out to read the 2nd and ended up reading them back to back. <br/><br/>In Lovely Trigger we find Danika sl</span>
  <span id="freeText11512287836410949535" style="display:none"><b>4.25 Second Chance Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394745176i/8899606._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">He'd set me adrift, so very long ago, and I had wandered into deepest waters, with depths far too vast for me to navigate alone.<br>And here he was, swimming out to save me. Had he been following me all the while? Had I been so blind?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394745176ra/8899607.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>What a perfect conclusion to the trilogy. It was emotional, angsty, erotic, everything you would want in a book. I waited until book 3 was out to read the 2nd and ended up reading them back to back. <br><br>In Lovely Trigger we find Danika slowly begin to pick up the pieces of her broken heart and shattered dreams. She has a job at James Cavendish's art gallery, and while she can't dance anymore, she gets by. As much as she tries to move on emotionally, she can never seem to fully forget the man that will always hold her heart.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I convinced myself that it had all been passion, not true love.  True love was a myth, a misdirection from the solid things in life.  What I’d felt for Tristan had been big and all consuming, but I told myself, like a mantra in my head, that it had never been solid.   Even so, every little thing brought him to mind.  We’d had too much together, been through too much, felt too much, and every feeling had a memory.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387940664ra/7702396.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She tries to move on, but no one ever compares to Tristan.<br><br>Tristan is dealing with his own demons. After hitting rock bottom, he's slowly but surely trying to climb his way out. He's gotten clean, a job as a magician in the Cavendish casino, but still the memory of Danika haunts him. He's riddled with guilt; for the things that he remembers and the things that he doesn't recall from his drugged out haze. Just reading about everything he went through after what happened in book 2 hit me right in the feels<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I didn’t trust myself, Danika. I needed my sobriety. I’m nothing without it, and you were a lovely trigger for me.  That look in your eyes, after all that I’d done…The way you looked at me like I was scum and knowing that I deserved all of your antipathy. I knew that if you looked at me like that again, I’d hit rock bottom, and this time I wouldn’t come back from it."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394833905ra/8913691.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I kept waiting for their reunion, knowing that when these two cross paths it will be explosive. And holy shit was it!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">The world stopped as we took what we needed, what I’d been starved for since the very last time I’d been in his arms.   It was a frenzied mating, a swift coming together that took me to the fever pitch of ecstasy with a few rough, heavy strokes, over too soon, the perfect testament to our torrid love affair.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394833905ra/8913692.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved the way that Tristan works to get back into Danika's heart again. You can feel his pain and heartache through the pages. As much as I wanted to hate him after the end of book 2, my heart went out to him. That's the beauty of a book written in dual first person POVs. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Love doesn't let you walk away clean. Love is messy. I don't have to tell you, of all people; Love takes a fucking piece of you before it's done."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>There was plenty of things stacked against them; their past, the secrets Danika still keeps, and their present. On a side note, Mona...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394833905ra/8913693.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was not as angsty as book 2, thankfully, but still packed a hell of a punch. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[When Danika finally reveals everything that happened that night to Tristan and reading his reaction? Gut-wrenching.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>But then there was that ending. <b>Perfection.</b> Not gonna lie, it brought a tear to my cold and black little heart. It was <b>that</b> good.<br><br>Why not 5 stars?<br>There were some things that I wanted a little more resolution for. I'm a picky bitch, what can I do?<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[After everything that happened with Danika and her sister, I wanted to see what happened with their relationship. I don't remember her being mentioned after that whole Tristan fiasco. I loved that she had her half-brother now, but some resolution with Dahlia would have been great. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Aside from that very minor thing, I loved the book. Trilogies are not something I read as I tend to grow bored with the same couple after 2 books. TO be honest, when I saw that there was going to be 3 books instead of the 2 that I had assumed, I almost didn't read it. (I blame my book ADD) But after reading these books I can definitely understand the necessity of it being stretched into 3. The story would not have been the same in just 2 books. Considering that this is my 2nd trilogy that I finished, it tells you something. If you love angsty, emotional, break-your-heart-then-put-it-back-together-with-a-cherry-on-top love stories, you need to read this.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389647314ra/8045566.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436206i/881587.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Kelli C " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c"><img alt="Kelli C " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1426900480p2/14931216.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/830792028?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelli C " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelli C " href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c">Kelli C </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=steamy-read">steamy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=second-chance-love">second-chance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=lovers-and-fighters">lovers-and-fighters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer830792028" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5503061070097215873">4.5 long way home stars!<br/><br/><b>“You don't need to follow every impulse in life; you don't need to take on every gamble. But some, even ones that have burned you before, well some of them you do. Some of the sweetest moments in life come from second chances.”</b><br/><br/>For Danika and Tristan neither horrific tragedy or long time spans apart could break the inherent love and passion they had for one another. <br/>Can one truly ever get forgiveness if they cannot find it within themselves?<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395185469i/8962666.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Tristan literally hit his rock b</span>
  <span id="freeText5503061070097215873" style="display:none">4.5 long way home stars!<br><br><b>“You don't need to follow every impulse in life; you don't need to take on every gamble. But some, even ones that have burned you before, well some of them you do. Some of the sweetest moments in life come from second chances.”</b><br><br>For Danika and Tristan neither horrific tragedy or long time spans apart could break the inherent love and passion they had for one another. <br>Can one truly ever get forgiveness if they cannot find it within themselves?<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395185469i/8962666.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Tristan literally hit his rock bottom when he lost his entire reason to live, his true light, his Danika. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395185469i/8962667._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Danika was always a survivor...she may not have wanted to live without her heart, but she would pick herself up and go on. She would live everyday with her wall built around her heart. But how can you not look into the eyes of Tristan Vega and not be consumed? <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395185469ra/8962668.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Time has matured both, it has scarred over old wounds, and it has given both new leases on life. What it has not done was stop their hearts from beating for one another. No one could make them smile and laugh the same, no one could challenge and accept a dare the same, and no one could create that amazing heat and intimate marathons the same.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395185469i/8962669._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I was so deeply invested in this couple that I felt every agonizing moment of uncertainty, every gut-wrenching flash from the past, and I was lost in every sinful touch that consumed them. I have never rooted so hard for a Second Chance...No couple has ever deserved happiness more than Tristan and Danika.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395185647i/8962697.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Again, this was not a pretty series... it was not flowers and sunshine. No, it was raw and gritty. It was a tale of consuming romance filled with blinding passion and harsh consequences. Lovely Trigger was a fabulously rough conclusion to a long hard road leading to pure happiness.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5503061070097215873" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5757800679306668502"><b>LOVED!</b> This whole series was a wild roller coaster of emotions. There was so much angst that I was near panic attacks and so enraged at certain points that I wanted to burn my own house down Carrie style. I really liked the Up In The Air Series by this author, but the Tristan and Danika books blew those away. There was just so much wonderful drama that it kept me on the edge of my seat and thinking about this story every waking minute. I can't stress how good these books are. They were hot and p</span>
  <span id="freeText5757800679306668502" style="display:none"><b>LOVED!</b> This whole series was a wild roller coaster of emotions. There was so much angst that I was near panic attacks and so enraged at certain points that I wanted to burn my own house down Carrie style. I really liked the Up In The Air Series by this author, but the Tristan and Danika books blew those away. There was just so much wonderful drama that it kept me on the edge of my seat and thinking about this story every waking minute. I can't stress how good these books are. They were hot and passionate, crazy and jealousy-inducing, tragic and horrifying, sad and heartbreaking, loving and forgiving. This series has it all! Tristan is just wonderful; I love everything about him. <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395032990i/8937930.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>He simply adores Danika and would do anything for her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395032990i/8937931._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All the wasted time that they lost is hard to handle. That is just something you cannot get back. Realizing the manipulations that occurred to damage them was gut-wrenching, as well. I loved every single word of this series even if it caused great pain and anguish, because at least the author was making me feel strong emotion. That is the most important thing I ask for in a book. This story, I know, will stay with me for a long time. I highly recommend this wild journey!<br><br><b>
  <i>"You don't need to follow every impulse in life; you don't need to take on every gamble. But some, even ones that have burned you before, well, some of them you do. Some of the sweetest moments in life come from second chances."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395032990i/8937932._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_882396661" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/882396661" />
    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/882396661?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=unable-to-put-down">unable-to-put-down</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=second-chances">second-chances</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=hot-as-hell">hot-as-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=best-of-2014">best-of-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer882396661" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3710043382725646875">~~~~ 5 SECOND CHANCE STARS! ~~~~<br/><br/>Wow! What a whirlwind of a series! Honestly, I don't know if I would have felt so acutely relieved and happy had I read this as each book was released. After reading Rock Bottom, I knew I made the right decision by waiting for all the books before starting this series. <br/>I went from happiness to sharp and depressing pain, followed by heartache and resignation, only to be woken up with a giddiness only an HEA could bring. And boy, did Tristan and Danika deserve a cha</span>
  <span id="freeText3710043382725646875" style="display:none">~~~~ 5 SECOND CHANCE STARS! ~~~~<br /><br />Wow! What a whirlwind of a series! Honestly, I don't know if I would have felt so acutely relieved and happy had I read this as each book was released. After reading Rock Bottom, I knew I made the right decision by waiting for all the books before starting this series. <br />I went from happiness to sharp and depressing pain, followed by heartache and resignation, only to be woken up with a giddiness only an HEA could bring. And boy, did Tristan and Danika deserve a chance at an HEA. Second chances are so sweet, bittersweet even, but ultimately satisfying beyond belief.<br /><br />Lovely Trigger was by far my favorite. Bad Things was bittersweet, Rock Bottom was achingly depressing, but this book was JOY. I knew after reading Grounded, the final book in this authors Up In The Air series, that Tristan and Danika had a whopping, epic love story. You could feel it just from the brief glimpses mentioned by Bianca. I had no idea their story was so profoundly affecting, so moving.<br /><br />Tristan. The boy had loads to make up for. I didn't like him much by the end of Rock Bottom, although I did feel sorry for his utter downward spiral into hell. How do you get back from that? Well, we got our answer! But here, holy crap! Here, he was the poster boy for redemption. His maturity, ability to single-mindedly focus on getting Danika back was admirable. He was impossibly sweet and determined! I teared up so many times reading how he felt about her, his losses and regrets. So many scenes were acutely tender and raw with his pain. <br /><br />And poor Danika, she felt she had moved on, or told herself that, but she was suffering under the infinite weight of denial. But together, finally being able to feel what each meant to the other....BEAUTIFUL. So many memorable parts: the cinnamon dare in Tristan's kitchen, the truth game at Danika's house....I felt their friendship and magic just by being together come off the pages.<br />And the steam? WOW. WOW. WOW. <br /><br />Steam is a usual part of romance these days, but it all blends into each other lately for me. Except here. Here, it's electrifying, powerful and incredibly sensual. The last 10% I was slobbering like a baby, refusing to do anything else but finish this book! It was addictive and scary and profound all at the same time. I loved the tenderness and pain from each word. Tristan, there are no words.... Freakin loved you!<br /><br />And Mona? Words are wasted on a skank like you. <br /><br />And the epilogue? my God. Can anything end so perfectly, so satisfyingly? LOVED, LOVED IT! This has been my Tristan and Danika weekend. And this book has made its way into my favourites pile!! Memorable and perfect, loved it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3710043382725646875" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_772799266" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/772799266" />
    <a title="Lisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5268966-lisa"><img alt="Lisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515253439p2/5268966.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/772799266?book_show_action=true">Nov 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/5268966-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5268966-lisa?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5268966-lisa?shelf=march">march</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer772799266" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9787002207629393948">I read this series in one sitting. To say my brain is oozing out my ears from the roller coaster ride I just got off of would be an understatement.<br/><br/>Many issues I reference are being put under the spoiler tag since I am dealing with specifics. Do not read if you haven't read this book.<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[When I finished book two I was convinced Tristan and Danika were <b>very</b> toxic together. The traumatic experiences they went through weren't handled well by either of them. Tristan was in self destruct mo</span></span>
  <span id="freeText9787002207629393948" style="display:none">I read this series in one sitting. To say my brain is oozing out my ears from the roller coaster ride I just got off of would be an understatement.<br /><br />Many issues I reference are being put under the spoiler tag since I am dealing with specifics. Do not read if you haven't read this book.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[When I finished book two I was convinced Tristan and Danika were <b>very</b> toxic together. The traumatic experiences they went through weren't handled well by either of them. Tristan was in self destruct mode for basically the whole book and Danika was going way beyond the role of enabler.<br /><br />When book three picks up everyone is trying to piece their lives back together. I admit I had serious issues with Tristan. Basically I initially felt he got off easy. I changed my mind on that position the more I got his point of view. He owned his shit (for lack of a better term). As with most addicts it takes a life changing event to have a come to Jesus moment. He took the steps to better his life and take full responsibility for his role with everything that happened with Danika. He asked for forgiveness and went about making a life without her. I like that time was spent getting into his head. Reading of the pain he was dealing with over the loss of Danika but having the strength to finally ask again and again to be a part of her life was heartwarming The downside for me was he still had serious anger issues where she was concerned. The jealousy behavior was ridiculous. After all the therapy he had to not have dealt with that major part of his former destructive lifestyle seemed illogical. <br /><br />This brings me to Danika. Her role as enabler was tough to read as the story unfolded. I wanted to yell more than once for her to 'woman up' and walk away. Love makes you blind but it also can make you deaf, dumb and stupid. I chalked it up to her young age. As we got a glimpse into her life 'after Tristan' she had a made a life for herself and accepting the cards she was dealt. What was hard for me was as time went on I was a screaming <b> 'get some therapy!!!'</b> again and again. Where Tristan was in a healthier place, Danika wasn't. It was hard to read. I was frustrated that no one in her circle suggested it. I felt it would have helped make this story more realistic. It would have shown growth on her part to take the steps to become mentally and emotionally healthy.<br /><br />Once Tristan and Danika were spending time together they seemed to fall back into the same roles: Sex makes everything better. That made me nuts. The lack of any real conversation and putting everything on the table to deal with the past was what was needed. Instead, as with prior books, they used sex as a way of communication. It felt like overkill. I needed more conversation. This was the area that they didn't seem to have matured. Why face reality when you can use sex. If they had gone to counseling together and talked about their history and dealt with everything it would have felt like a natural progression. <br /><br />Did I enjoy seeing how their love was the underlying current to their HEA? Yes. When they <b><i> FINALLY</i></b> had the extremely sad and emotionally draining conversation where everything was finally dealt with I let out a sigh of relief. The reality that she couldn't have children and Tristan's reaction broke my heart. It was maddening that we had to wait until roughly the last 20% mark for this to happen though. After everything I needed more time spent on this area. (I will say I was completely baffled that NO ONE told Danika that since she had her ovaries she still had eggs. WTF? Her going through life thinking she had no options seemed like it was just a ploy to make her story that much more dramatic when it wasn't necessary). <br />(Plus don't get me started on Tristan donating sperm to Frankie. WTF!)<br /><br />The ending felt like someone sprinkled fairy dust everywhere and things were all rainbows and unicorns. While sweet, I felt something was missing. It felt like after the huge amounts of pain and heartache making their life TOTALLY PERFECT wasn't realistic. <br /><br />In closing, please note I <b>am not</b> bashing this series. I applaud R.K. Lilley for taking me on such an emotional ride. I was glued to this story from start to finish for two days. I ran through a bucket load of emotions. Am I glad I read this series? Yes. Am I on the bandwagon like a majority of the other readers, unfortunately No but that's ok.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Thank you Whitney for holding my hand as I read (and complained and fussed and rambled) this series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9787002207629393948" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText12069083139352124857" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"How can we be so good for each other in so many ways, and so bad in just as many others?"</b>
</blockquote><br>If you haven't started this series I don't know what you're waiting for, but you need to get to it.<br>This book was everything I could've asked for and even more. This review is being typed in the midst of tears and wine. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800287i/667095.png" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393553i/757717.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"We were rushing headlong into this lunacy, and I could worry about the mess we made later."</b><br><br>Tristan and Danika's story is: <br><i>Heartbreaking<br>Beautiful<br>Real<br>Sexy <br>Satisfactory</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394668497i/8886344.png" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I feel as if this couple are friends of mine and I've witnessed their journey from the beginning to end. The saga of Tristan and Danika has sadly come to an end. I laughed, cried, got angry from book one to three. This book picks up years after the explosive events in book two. Tristan is a changed man and Danika has found the strength to pick up the pieces and move on. Oh how I wish I could say more, but this review will be kept purposefully short and spoiler free.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800287i/667095.png" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6574132.R_K__Lilley" title="R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">R.K. Lilley</a> has written a story that will remain in my heart for a long time. Simply amazing. I will never be able to adequately convey the depth of emotion and deep connection this couple share, so I'll use Tristan's words to end this review.<br><br><b>From Tristan to Danika</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>Remember when you told me that I was yours and you were mine<br>Every heartbeat, every breath,<br>Our love was perfect, our vows were sacred<br>and, oh sweetheart, you know I tried so hard to tow that line,<br>But there was a poison in my heart,<br>And a darkness in my mind<br>I wasn't there when you were drowning<br>Though I'd give my soul to take it back <br>You had to leave me behind<br>Looking back, over the years of empty space,<br>Through the harshest rearview mirror,<br>Remembering the things I put you through<br>Now left to wonder, who's come to take my place<br>When I looked at you the world dissolved <br>My poison cured, my darkness light<br>I never did deserve you, sweetheart<br>But in your arms my wrongs were solved</i>

<span id="freeTextContainer13438984666721045169"><b>4.5 Stars!</b><br/><br/>This is the final book in Tristan and Danika's love story.<br/><br/>In the start of this book, we get a recap on what has been going on in Tristan and Danika's lives over the last six years. Tristan has finally decided he has waited around long enough for Danika and he wants to be in her life again, even if they can only be friends. They have so many past hurts that they may never be able to truly be together but Tristan is clean and sober now and he wants a chance to prove that he is better tha</span>
  <span id="freeText13438984666721045169" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars!</b><br><br>This is the final book in Tristan and Danika's love story.<br><br>In the start of this book, we get a recap on what has been going on in Tristan and Danika's lives over the last six years. Tristan has finally decided he has waited around long enough for Danika and he wants to be in her life again, even if they can only be friends. They have so many past hurts that they may never be able to truly be together but Tristan is clean and sober now and he wants a chance to prove that he is better than he ever was. He has his life straight, but can Danika forgive him for all of the hurt that he caused?<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395008700ra/8935030.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395008700ra/8935031.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Danika is very stubborn. She doesn't completely trust Tristan anymore, but it is so hard to stay away from him. They have always been drawn together and that definitely hasn't changed over the years. After finally agreeing to being friends again, she realizes how much she has truly missed just being around him.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395008700ra/8935032.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>His eyes were twinkling; he couldn't stop smiling. "You know I adore you, but there are times when I just like to torture you. It makes me happy." ~Tristan</i>
</b><br><br><br>There are so many things for them to try and work through, things that Tristan needs Danika to tell him because he doesn't remember.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395008700ra/8935033.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395008700ra/8935034.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer879085294" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16153128658928135902">A heart-wrenching finale to Tristan and Danika's story. This series made me laugh, cry and want to throw things in fury. I absolutely couldn't get enough of their love story. After the tragic endings in books 1 and 2, I was really worried that book 3 was going to end with some other great tragedy. I'm glad to say that wasn't the case. While the events of the past can't be undone, this story is about the ability of love to conquer all. It is definitely one of my new favorites. Loved it!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_877924474" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/877924474" />
    <a title="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13629682-ang-sizzling-pages"><img alt="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1541857150p2/13629682.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/877924474?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" href="/user/show/13629682-ang-sizzling-pages">Ang (Sizzling Pages)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940149364466" href="/book/show/18681461-lovely-trigger">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13629682-ang-sizzling-pages?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer877924474" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3048029906578759255">5 Amazing Stars<br/>Arc provided by author in exchange for an honest review<br/>For more reviews, please visit <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.sizzlingpages.com'>www.sizzlingpages.com</a><br/><br/><a href='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XpR9jSmq1xE/Uy4gazDdSKI/AAAAAAAAE6k/lPQQp9h7V9g/s1600/images.jpeg' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395546160i/9012829._SX540_.jpg' height='428' width='640' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
    
</a><br/><br/>Met you through Mr. Cavendish. You were a mysterious, sexy, arrogant, larger than life character with a humongous ego to match… Had the feeling you held secrets and I was itching to know your story.<br/><br/>In Bad Things, you proved your arrogance. You were such a dawg. A manwhore. And I knew you were trouble from the very beginning. You’re just another playa, stringing along</span>
  <span id="freeText3048029906578759255" style="display:none">5 Amazing Stars<br>Arc provided by author in exchange for an honest review<br>For more reviews, please visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.sizzlingpages.com">www.sizzlingpages.com</a><br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XpR9jSmq1xE/Uy4gazDdSKI/AAAAAAAAE6k/lPQQp9h7V9g/s1600/images.jpeg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395546160i/9012829._SX540_.jpg" height="428" width="640" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
    
</a><br><br>Met you through Mr. Cavendish. You were a mysterious, sexy, arrogant, larger than life character with a humongous ego to match… Had the feeling you held secrets and I was itching to know your story.<br><br>In Bad Things, you proved your arrogance. You were such a dawg. A manwhore. And I knew you were trouble from the very beginning. You’re just another playa, stringing along a beautiful girl, setting her up for heartache.<br><br>You hit Rock Bottom and I was gutted. Your life was tail spinning, spiraling out of control. Tristan, you filleted my heart and tore me to shreds. How could you?? I was totally frustrated and MAJORLY pissed off when you abandoned all sense of reason and surrendered to the demons that haunted you. For such a powerful man, your weaknesses took hold, the ghosts from your past held their victory, and you lost the one shinning light that graced your existence. You did a fine job of setting yourself up for a future laced deep emotional darkness. I could smack the shit outta you.<br>But, all the while, I adored you. You magically casted a spell over me using your animalistic sex appeal and charisma. I did not stand a chance. <br><br>And now…BEHOLD! The powerful force that is Tristan pieces himself together and from feebleness comes strength. Like the phoenix rising from cinders, Tristan is reborn. Now clean and sober, he is placing the broken pieces of his shattered life back together, save one – Danika. Losing her left Tristan incomplete and empty. Living without his love for over six years, is not a life worth living. And now he is determined to get her back, no matter how long it takes.<br><br><br><a href="http://24.media.tumblr.com/d58d81264344288ba1dbca4f18c51bf5/tumblr_msxe9tUliW1sg3u26o1_500.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385965301ra/7266550.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Z9pwm1nhXOI/Uy5G9EpLnMI/AAAAAAAAE7k/GGZt3LLdVog/s1600/78d99934acea549c6f8f9c572b09b66b.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395546160i/9012830._SY540_.jpg" height="400" width="362" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <i>
  <b>
    Even if I couldn’t be her husband, I longed to have her in my life.  In any capacity.  I’d take literally anything. I wouldn’t be happy with less than everything, but I’d take what I could get. Crumbs, scraps, tastes of what she once felt for me, as a salve for what I still felt in abundance for her. 
  </b>
</i><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bR9ykeGn5ec/Uy5FKtGo9mI/AAAAAAAAE7U/8hjL8lNsEjM/s1600/0ead2edf26e776b342a1314a553f3f7e.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395546160i/9012831._SY540_.jpg" height="400" width="273" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><b>
  
    “Because that’s how love works.  
    It doesn’t die, even when you don’t feed it.
      
    That’s just the way it is.
      
    I wouldn’t change it, even if I could.
      
    Loving her has become a part of who I am.”
  
</b><br><br>Lovely Trigger, the long anticipated final installment to the Tristan and Danika Series, is a tale of hope, redemption, forgiveness and an undying love that burns within the hearts of two broken souls. Trust me, these two are quite dysfunctional…<br><br>I was immediately sucked into the Tristan and Danika's saga. I became obsessively addicted to the drama that surrounded their lives, passions, heartaches and desires. Their erotic tale was so filled with angst, I loved every nail biting, heart stopping, soul gutting moment. RK Lilley set me on a roller-coaster ride that left me whirling and twisted my emotions as if being swept away by a violent tornado. This series was sizzling.<br><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="https://p.gr-assets.com/540x540/fit/hostedimages/1387935431/7701534.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387935431ra/7701534.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><br><br>Metaphorically speaking, I define Tristan and Danika’s relationship as <i>magnetic</i>. Two poles: one side drawing them together, their attraction is undeniable and the bond is everlasting.  On the flip side: the circumstances that evolve around their lives exert a force so powerful, like similar poles of a magnet, repelling and totally annihilating each other to the point of devastation.<br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Da3vX_HqB04/Uy4eVddsYPI/AAAAAAAAE6Y/gS7SHp91Br8/s1600/Sad.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395546160i/9012832._SX540_.jpg" height="265" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>To fully appreciate the true beauty of their tumultuous love story, one needs to understand Tristan’s pain. A darkness consumes his soul, the demons that torcher him affects Danika and becomes the root of her pain as well. These demons are the catalyst for all the heartache, which befalls this couple. The turmoil with in him wreaks havoc in their lives. Tristan’s actions causes him to do the unforgivable - utterly destroying Danika’s life.  He infuriated me to no end with his lack of control.<br><br>BUT, as much as I wanted to be angry with Tristan and rip his head off because of all the hurtful shit he pulled, he always held my heart.  Here lies his beauty.  Despite how his selfish actions caused Danika ‘’s anguish, he truly loved her.  And his love was so strong, it gave him the fortitude to turn his life around.  It gave him the courage to clean up his act and pull Danika from the depths of despair.  This was no easy task, for Danika removed herself from his life for years. However long it took to pave his way back into her life, he would serve his penance because he can no longer live with out his woman.<br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-eBf4oOicXTk/UyGTRSZ_nyI/AAAAAAAAE5w/qx7FtluXbaQ/s1600/Megan_Fox.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395546160i/9012833._SY540_.jpg" height="400" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Danika is empty, joyless.  Tristan decimated and destroyed her life, leaving her body and soul barren.  Her existence was dismal. Closing herself off, building impenetrable walls around her heart, Danika barely manages to survive.  Her focus is her career and little else. And yes, her heart still belongs to Tristan and thoughts of him dominate her mind. For several painful years, Danika was nothing more than an empty shell. Until one unguarded moment, she succumbs to unbridled passion, and gifts herself the pleasure of all things Tristan. She devours him. Feelings of love and longing take control, and needless to say these two create heat that will melt your panties off. It’s just the crack in her armor that Tristan prayed for in his quest to regain Danika.<br>As much as she hates how Tristan ruined her life, she adores him to no end.  No man will own her heart for Tristan is her soul mate as much as he is her destroyer.  Her love for him runs so deep, she alone carries the burden of truth as to the events which occurred that ill fated night, when all Danika treasured was violently ripped away.  She is incapable of disclosing the truth for fear of destroying him further… eventually, all is revealed.  And Tristan’s reaction is anything but predicable. When discovering how his poison leaked and turned Danika’s world upside down, he persevered and worked harder to solidify their relationship. Tristan became was unwavering and in full control of their destiny.  FINALLY, Tristan manned-up.<br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-aqm2o1Cgyyw/Uy5FL3ifD4I/AAAAAAAAE7c/6ofpPG3_xe4/s1600/b10791adb2076318193932fa51956add.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395546160i/9012835._SY540_.jpg" height="400" width="265" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  
    “Oh Danika,” he said softly. 
    I started shaking my head vehemently. 
    “Tell me, sweetheart.  Whatever it is, I’ll fix it.”
    I closed my eyes, my face crumbling. 
    “Oh sweetheart,” he said, softer now, closer now. 
    “I feel so lost.”
    He took my hands in his. 
    “Not anymore.  I’m right here.  I’ve got you.” 
    “There is this hollow place inside of me, where my faith in you used to be. 
    I am so full of fear, and I do not know how to let myself trust you again. 
    I don’t have the strength to do this.  Not again.” 
    “I’ve got enough for both of us.”  He moved closer, wrapping me in his arms. 
  
  
    “It’s about time I got a turn letting you lean on me.”   
  
   
</i>Of course, there were some bitches that tried to derail their relationship all I can say to them is….<br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://img.pandawhale.com/99785-Fuck-you-gif-Elsa-Disney-froze-UfwS.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394927914ra/8925668.gif" height="172" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://img.pandawhale.com/post-34672-I-wont-take-this-bullshit-anym-MqFT.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395546160ra/9012836.gif" height="285" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div>Tristan’s character fascinated me from the moment he was first introduce in the <i>“Up in the Air” series</i>. I was totally intrigued by how his persona morphed from a selfish, self-centered man – to a selfless man so desperate to repair the two lives he destroyed. It was remarkable.  He atoned for his sins by walking through hell, through the fire and made it to the other side.  Setting a new and better course for his life, he was redeemed and unwavering in his need to bring Danika healing and peace. As much as she tried to fight the pull towards Tristan, he never gave up.  And she had no choice but to give in. They were meant to be together. And he gave everything to assure their future would be filled with bliss. That’s where Tristan won me over.  That and the fact that he’s an unbelievably sexy dirty talking bastard – it was impossible for me NOT to love him.<br><div>
<br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-muOtj0wKKNg/Uy5MNOw2L0I/AAAAAAAAE70/SfWFss-cWCg/s1600/485045_552884678067097_1890933771_n.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395547006i/9012899.jpg" height="320" width="180" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</div><br><blockquote>
<br>It was official.  We’d been through hell, but here we were, in our own little slice of heaven.  </blockquote><br><br><br><div>
<br><a href="https://p.gr-assets.com/540x540/fit/hostedimages/1392255811/8527249.gif" rel="nofollow noopener"><img height="208" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392255811ra/8527249.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</div><br><div>
<br><br>
</div><br>Lovely Trigger was a bittersweet experience for me.  I had an unhealthy obsession of wanting to see their “happily ever after”.  But part of me never, ever wanted to let them go. Tristan and Danika’s journey, laced in gut wrenching pain, ended magnificently. RK is one of my favorite writers.  The masterful way she portrayed the love story of Tristan and Danika was amazing.  So happy to see them reach their well deserved happily ever after.<br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-eMABkq2btms/UxwRAFrN2wI/AAAAAAAAE4Q/-wPApFp-2OM/s1600/Metal+sig+Ang.png" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395547006i/9012900._SY540_.png" height="200" width="192" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><div><br></div></span>
  <a data-text-id="3048029906578759255" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
